## CAS Registry Number

### 3.2.S.1.1 Nomenclature and Regulatory Designations
#### 3.2.S.1.1.1 CAS Registry Number and Chemical Identification

**1. Primary CAS Registry Number Assignment**

The drug substance, Glucogen-XR (glucapeptide extended-release), produced by Google Health Sciences (GHS), has been assigned a unique Chemical Abstracts Service (CAS) Registry Number by the American Chemical Society (ACS) following a comprehensive structural review and validation of the recombinant peptide sequence and its associated post-translational modifications.

**CAS Registry Number: 2948572-14-8**

The assignment of this number is based on the specific amino acid sequence of the glucapeptide moiety and the proprietary extended-release linkage technology employed in the manufacturing process at the South San Francisco facility.

**Table 1.1.1-1: Summary of CAS Registration and Identification Data**

| Parameter | Specification / Value | Reference Standard |
| :--- | :--- | :--- |
| **CAS Registry Number** | 2948572-14-8 | ACS Registry Services |
| **CAS Index Name** | Glucagon-like peptide 1 (human), (2S)-2-amino-5-[[(1S)-1-carboxy-4-[[(1S)-1-carboxy-2-[[2-[2-[2-[[2-[2-[2-[[(19S)-19-carboxy-1-oxo-20-sulfoicosyl]amino]ethoxy]ethoxy]acetyl]amino]ethoxy]ethoxy]acetyl]amino]ethyl]amino]-4-oxobutyl]amino]-5-oxopentyl]- | IUPAC/IUBMB |
| **Molecular Formula** | $C_{198}H_{314}N_{48}O_{64}S_{2}$ | Theoretical Calculation |
| **Molecular Weight** | 4,524.12 Daltons (Average) | High-Resolution Mass Spectrometry (HRMS) |
| **USAN Name** | Glucapeptide Extended-Release | USP/NF |
| **INN Name** | Glucapeptidum prolongatum | WHO INN List 132 |

---

**2. Procedural Protocol for CAS Registry Verification (GHS-SOP-REG-0042)**

To ensure the integrity of the regulatory submissions and the accurate identification of Glucogen-XR across all manufacturing batches (e.g., GLUC-2025-001 through GLUC-2025-500), Google Health Sciences adheres to a strict verification protocol.

**Step-by-Step Procedure for Sequence Validation and CAS Submission:**

1.  **Primary Sequence Confirmation (LC-MS/MS):**
    *   Utilize the Agilent 6545XT AdvanceBio LC/Q-TOF.
    *   Perform tryptic digestion on the drug substance batch (e.g., Batch GLUC-2025-012).
    *   Map peptide fragments against the theoretical sequence derived from the GHS-CHO-001 cell line expression vector.
    *   *Calculation:* Percent Coverage = $\frac{\text{Observed Amino Acids}}{\text{Total Sequence Length}} \times 100$. Requirement: $\geq 99.5\%$.

2.  **Substructure Analysis for Linker Identification:**
    *   The extended-release C-terminal modification is verified via NMR spectroscopy (Bruker Avance III 600 MHz).
    *   Chemical shifts ($\delta$) are compared against the master reference standard (GHS-REF-GLUC-001).

3.  **Submission to ACS:**
    *   Electronically transmit the verified FASTA sequence and the chemical structure of the lipidated side chain to the Chemical Abstracts Service.
    *   Include a detailed description of the disulfide bridging (if applicable) and the sulfonation state of the C-20 icosyl group.

---

Each production batch manufactured at 3000 Innovation Drive undergoes a Quality Control (QC) check to ensure the chemical identity matches the CAS-registered profile.

---

**4. Regulatory Justification and Reference Standards**

The designation of CAS Number 2948572-14-8 is critical for compliance with the following regulatory frameworks:

*   **ICH Q6B:** Specifications: Test Procedures and Acceptance Criteria for Biotechnological/Biological Products. The CAS number serves as the primary chemical identifier in the Summary of Product Characteristics (SmPC).
*   **USP <1041>:** Biologics. Provides the framework for naming and chemical identification of recombinant peptides.
*   **FDA Guidance for Industry:** *Naming of Biological Products (2017)*. The use of a distinct CAS number facilitates the pharmacovigilance tracking of Glucogen-XR, distinguishing it from non-extended-release GLP-1 analogues.

**5. Detailed Chemical Structural Components Supporting CAS Assignment**

The CAS registry entry for Glucogen-XR accounts for three distinct structural domains:

1.  **Peptide Backbone:** A 31-amino acid sequence derived from the human proglucagon gene, expressed in the proprietary GHS-CHO-001 (GS knockout) cell line.
2.  **Spacer Unit:** A bis-aminodiethoxyacetyl (OEG) spacer linked to the Lysine residue at position 26.
3.  **Hydrophobic Anchor:** A C-20 fatty diacid (icosanedioic acid) with a terminal sulfonic acid group to enhance albumin binding and prolong half-life (XR properties).

**Statistical Calculation of Mass Variance across CAS-Registered Batches:**

To maintain the CAS identity, the molecular weight variance across 50 consecutive batches (GLUC-2025-001 to GLUC-2025-050) was analyzed:

$$\sigma^2 = \frac{\sum (X_i - \mu)^2}{n - 1}$$

Where:
*   $\mu$ (Mean Mass) = 4524.12 Da
*   $n$ = 50
*   Calculated Standard Deviation ($\sigma$) = 0.02 Da

This extremely low variance confirms the high level of process control maintained by Google Health Sciences and justifies the continued use of a single CAS Registry Number for the drug substance.

### 3.2.S.1.1.4 Drug Master File (DMF) References

This section provides a comprehensive and exhaustive accounting of all Drug Master Files (DMFs) incorporated by reference to support the New Drug Application (NDA) for Glucogen-XR (glucapeptide extended-release). Google Health Sciences (GHS) maintains Letters of Authorization (LOAs) for all third-party DMFs listed herein, confirming that the FDA has the necessary permissions to review the confidential technical information contained within these files in connection with this submission.

#### 1.0 Overview of DMF Strategy for Glucapeptide Extended-Release
The manufacturing of Glucogen-XR involves a complex global supply chain encompassing recombinant protein expression, sophisticated purification via chromatography, and a proprietary extended-release formulation utilizing advanced polymer science. To maintain the highest level of regulatory compliance and intellectual property protection, GHS utilizes a tiered DMF structure.

##### 1.1 Classification of Referenced DMFs
As per 21 CFR 314.420, the following classifications are utilized in this section:
*   **Type II:** Drug Substance, Drug Substance Intermediate, and Material Used in Their Preparation, or Drug Product.
*   **Type III:** Packaging Material.
*   **Type IV:** Excipient, Colorant, Flavor, Essence, or Material Used in Their Preparation.
*   **Type V:** FDA-Accepted Reference Material.

---

#### 2.0 Comprehensive List of DMF References (Technical Matrix)

The following table provides the primary index for all DMFs referenced in this Module 3.2.S submission. All LOAs are provided in Section 1.4.1 of this application.

| DMF Number | DMF Holder | Subject of DMF | DMF Type | Initial Filing Date | Most Recent Annual Report Date | Status |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :---: | :---: | :---: | :--- |
| **DMF 012884** | Google Cloud Bio-Materials | Proprietary CHO-K1 GS-Knockout Cell Line (GHS-CHO-001) | II | 12-JAN-2018 | 15-JAN-2024 | Active |
| **DMF 044921** | Polymer Dynamics Inc. | PEG-PLGA Block Copolymer (XR-Matrix Grade) | IV | 03-MAR-2021 | 10-FEB-2024 | Active |
| **DMF 099832** | Sigma-Millipore Biologics | Chemically Defined Media (CD-CHO-V3) | IV | 18-AUG-2015 | 22-SEP-2023 | Active |
| **DMF 022115** | West Pharmaceutical Services | FluroTec® Stopper Components | III | 05-JUN-2005 | 11-NOV-2023 | Active |

| **DMF 011004** | Global Resins & Catalysts | Proprietary Catalyst for Peptide Conjugation | IV | 09-JUL-2019 | 15-DEC-2023 | Active |

#### 3.0 Detailed Analysis of Type II DMF References (Drug Substance & Intermediates)

##### 3.1 DMF 012884: Proprietary CHO-K1 GS-Knockout Cell Line (GHS-CHO-001)
The Drug Substance, Glucapeptide, is expressed using the GHS-CHO-001 cell line. This DMF contains exhaustive details regarding the lineage, genetic engineering (CRISPR/Cas9 mediated Glutamine Synthetase knockout), and the stability of the expression vector over the calculated Limit of In Vitro Cell Age (LIVCA).

**3.1.1 Cell Bank Testing Protocols Referenced**
GHS references the following protocols within DMF 012884 to ensure the absence of adventitious agents and the maintenance of phenotypic stability:
1.  **Protocol GHS-CB-001:** Sterility testing via USP <71>.
2.  **Protocol GHS-CB-004:** Mycoplasma testing (Culture and DNA Fluorochrome methods) per USP <63>.
3.  **Protocol GHS-CB-009:** In-vitro and In-vivo viral screening (ICH Q5A).

**3.1.2 Batch Correlation Table (Master Cell Bank / Working Cell Bank)**
The following batches of Glucapeptide (Glucogen-XR) were produced using cell banks characterized under DMF 012884:

| Glucogen-XR Batch ID | Cell Bank Lot (WCB) | Fermentation Scale (L) | Yield (g/L) | Date of Completion |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |
| GLUC-2025-001 | WCB-GHS-001-A | 2,000L | 4.22 | 12-JAN-2025 |
| GLUC-2025-002 | WCB-GHS-001-A | 2,000L | 4.35 | 25-JAN-2025 |
| GLUC-2025-003 | WCB-GHS-001-B | 2,000L | 4.18 | 08-FEB-2025 |

---

#### 4.0 Detailed Analysis of Type IV DMF References (Excipients & Catalysts)

##### 4.1 DMF 044921: PEG-PLGA Block Copolymer (XR-Matrix Grade)
The extended-release profile of Glucogen-XR is achieved through encapsulation in a biodegradable PEG-PLGA (polyethylene glycol-poly(lactic-co-glycolic acid)) matrix. The synthesis, molecular weight distribution, and residual solvent profile of this polymer are proprietary to Polymer Dynamics Inc.

**4.1.1 Critical Quality Attributes (CQAs) defined in DMF 044921:**
*   **Lactide:Glycolide Ratio:** 50:50 ± 2% (determined by NMR).
*   **Inherent Viscosity:** 0.45 - 0.55 dL/g.
*   **Glass Transition Temperature (Tg):** 42°C - 48°C.
*   **Polydispersity Index (PDI):** ≤ 1.8.

**4.1.2 Integration into Glucogen-XR Manufacturing Process**
The polymer is dissolved in a solvent system (Reference DMF 011004 for Catalyst details) before being subjected to the proprietary Google Cloud Life Sciences Microfluidic Encapsulation (GCLS-ME) process.

**Mathematical Formula for Encapsulation Efficiency (EE%):**
$$EE\% = \frac{(Total\ Glucapeptide\ added - Free\ non-encapsulated\ peptide)}{Total\ Glucapeptide\ added} \times 100$$

**Encapsulation Data per Batch:**
| Batch ID | Polymer Lot | Target EE% | Actual EE% | Release Rate (Day 7) |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |
| GLUC-2025-101 | PD-2024-88 | >95% | 98.2% | 14.2% |
| GLUC-2025-102 | PD-2024-88 | >95% | 97.9% | 13.8% |
| GLUC-2025-103 | PD-2024-92 | >95% | 98.5% | 14.5% |

---

#### 5.0 Quality Control and Compliance with DMF Holders

##### 5.1 Vendor Qualification Program (Protocol VQP-GHS-2025)
All DMF holders listed are subject to the Google Health Sciences Vendor Qualification Program. This program ensures that the data provided in the DMFs align with our internal quality control (QC) testing of incoming raw materials.

**Step-by-Step Procedure for Incoming Raw Material Validation (Procedure SOP-QC-0044):**
1.  **Verification:** Verify that the CoA (Certificate of Analysis) matches the specifications listed in the referenced DMF.
2.  **Sampling:** Sample material in an ISO Class 5 laminar flow hood using sterile, pyrogen-free equipment.
3.  **Identity Testing:** Perform FT-IR or NIR spectroscopy to confirm chemical identity against the reference standard established in DMF 044921.
4.  **Purity Analysis:** Conduct HPLC or GC analysis for residual monomers/solvents as specified in the "Confidential Section" of the DMF.
5.  **Microbial Limits:** Test for TAMC (Total Aerobic Microbial Count) and TYMC (Total Yeast and Mold Count) per USP <61>.
